Hays moved to the #LehighValley as a child &amp; always considered Allentown her home. Her rank &amp; military accolades made her eligible for a burial at @ArlingtonNatl, but she opted for her final resting place to be South Whitehall Twp, here at home.
It's impossible to convey in a single tweet thread the breadth of Hays legacy, both as a military pioneer for female service members and as a compassionate medical professional.
